### All the decisions have a non WTT dependent and a WTT version.

economy_decisions = {
	SOV_replace_baku_with_volga_ural_basin = { #accelerate oil decisions if lost azerbaijan
		
		icon = oil

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}
		highlight_states = {
			state = 249
		}
		available = {
			has_tech = excavation2
			owns_state = 249
			controls_state = 249
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 5			
			NOT = {
				has_idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
				controls_state = 229
			}			
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 229
				has_tech = excavation_a
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 100
		days_remove = 210

		modifier = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
				days = 120
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		remove_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = prospect_volga_ural_basin
		}	
	}

	expand_the_ljubija_iron_mine = { #824 #iron mine in Bosnia
		
		icon = steel #change if copper is added

		allowed = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
    				has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
			}
		}
		highlight_states = {
			state = 824
		}
		available = {
			has_tech = excavation2
			owns_state = 824
			controls_state = 824
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2			
			NOT = {
				has_idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
			}			
		}

		visible = {
			owns_state = 824
			controls_state = 824
			824 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = open_ljubija_mine_developed
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 17
		days_remove = 180

		modifier = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
				days = 60
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				steel < 5
			}			
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				steel < 1
			}			
		}
		remove_effect = { 
			824 = { set_state_flag = open_ljubija_mine_developed } 
			824 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 5
				}
			}
		}	
	}

		allowed = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
    				has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
			}
		}
		highlight_states = {
			state = 492
		}
		available = {
			has_tech = excavation2
			owns_state = 289
			controls_state = 289
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 3
			NOT = {
				has_idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
			}			
		}

		visible = {
			owns_state = 289
			controls_state = 289
			289 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = siamese_tungsten_exploited
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 80


		modifier = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
				days = 35
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				tungsten < 10
			}			
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				tungsten < 5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				date > 1943.01.01
			}			
		}
		remove_effect = { 
			289 = { set_state_flag = siamese_tungsten_exploited } 
			289 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = tungsten
					amount = 8
				}
			}
		}	
	}

	expand_cuban_chromium = { # 
		
		icon = chromium

		allowed = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
    				has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
			}			
		}

		available = {
			owns_state = 315
			controls_state = 315
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 6
			has_tech = excavation4
			NOT = {
				has_idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
			}			
		}
		highlight_states = {
			state = 315
		}

		visible = {
			owns_state = 315
			controls_state = 315
			315 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = { 
						flag = cuban_chromium_expanded 
						value = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 60

		complete_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
				days = 30
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				chromium < 5
			}			
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				chromium < 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				date > 1942.01.01
			}			
		}
		remove_effect = { 
			add_to_variable = { var = cuban_chromium_duration value = 30 }
			315 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = cuban_chromium_expanded
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = {
						flag = cuban_chromium_expanded
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					modify_state_flag = {
						flag = cuban_chromium_expanded
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}		
			315 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = chromium
					amount = 10
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = cuban_chromium_duration value = 30 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = cuban_chromium_duration value = 30 }
			}
		}		
	}

		remove_effect = {

						}

					set_state_flag = {
						flag = marcona_iron_exploited
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {

						flag = marcona_iron_exploited
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}				
			492 = {
				add_resource = {

					amount = 8
				}
			}
		}

						flag = north_carolina_tungsten_developed 
						value = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 15
		days_remove = USA_north_carolina_tungsten_duration

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 10
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = USA_north_carolina_tungsten_duration value = 30 }
			363 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = north_carolina_tungsten_developed
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = {
						flag = north_carolina_tungsten_developed
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					modify_state_flag = {
						flag = north_carolina_tungsten_developed
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			363 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = tungsten
					amount = 8
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				tungsten < 5
			}			
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				tungsten < 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				date > 1943.01.01
			}				
			modifier = {
				has_political_power < 200
				add = -4
			}			
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = USA_north_carolina_tungsten_duration value = 30 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = USA_north_carolina_tungsten_duration value = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
